Jiading 82

Another Robbery Case in the Western Countryside: At about 1:00 AM on the 12th, more than 20 robbers suddenly broke into the house of Shen Wende, a farmer in Shenjiaku Village near Anting Town in the county, and committed a robbery. The entire family was tied up with ropes and threatened into silence. They stole more than 300 yuan in silver dollars, 18 shi of white rice, as well as clothing, jewelry, cloth, preserved meat, bedding, and other miscellaneous items. By the time the town's security team heard the alarm and rushed to the scene, the bandits had fled far away. According to the victim, the bandits spoke with a Jiangbei accent and seemed to be people working on boats nearby. The case has been reported to the county for investigation.

Fengxian 83

Mediation of Electricity Price Increase Dispute: Recently, the Nanqiao Lixiang Power Plant increased the price per lamp by 2 fen starting in February to subsidize the soaring oil prices. However, the users demanded that the lights be repaired first before they could agree to the price increase, resulting in a major conflict between the two parties. Although the county party department and others repeatedly negotiated to reduce the electricity price by 1 fen, the matter was not resolved due to the users raising the issue of installing electricity meters. They are now firmly refusing to use electricity, expressing their determination. The power plant has also stopped supplying electricity to those households who have not paid the overdue fees, causing the trend between the two parties to become increasingly serious. The county government fears that if this stalemate continues, there may be dangerous consequences in the future, so it has formulated appropriate conditions at this county government meeting and will convene both parties again tomorrow by County Magistrate Shen to persuade them.

A Woman Committed Suicide in Anger Due to Giving Birth to a Deformed Child: Chen, a woman from Shijiazhuang Fentou Village, west of Daijiaqiao in the county, suddenly gave birth to a deformed child the day before yesterday. The child's face was swollen like jade, its hands and feet were connected, and its cry was as faint as a mosquito. The news spread far and wide, and crowds gathered to watch. The ignorant even regarded it as an ominous sign. As a result, the woman, ashamed and angry, committed suicide by taking poison last night.

Nanhui 84

Election of Labor Union Representatives to the National Assembly: Yesterday, the Zhoupu Match Factory Labor Union and the Xinchang Zhao Weaving Factory Labor Union simultaneously voted to elect representatives to the National Assembly in the third and eighth district offices. The results of the ballot count showed that Cao Pinru, Hui Chunzhi, Wang Jianqiu, Zhang Hentian, Chen Changgeng, and Qiu Liqi received the most votes and were reported to the county on the same day.

Ling Xibai Was Falsely Accused of Colluding with Bandits: Ling Xibai, who has been a primary school teacher, was suddenly accused by Huang Jingchu, a person from Liuzao Town, of colluding with bandits to kidnap the son of the late wealthy household Huang Yongqing in Chenqiao Town for ransom. The Jiangsu Pacification Supervisor's Office was asked to detain him for investigation. The office ordered the county to thoroughly investigate the matter, and the county government issued a warrant for arrest and interrogation. Subsequently, Jun Ji and Xie Xing, merchants, and others stated that Ling Xibai had been working in the education sector and was honest and reliable, and it was clear that he had been falsely accused due to a grudge. They jointly requested a thorough investigation. The county ordered the sixth district office to investigate and report the facts. Yesterday, the office replied that Ling Xibai had been a primary school teacher in Yaodun Village in the second district, was law-abiding, and had no suspicion of colluding with bandits. It was also found that there was no such person as Huang Jingchu in Liuzao Town, and it was undoubtedly a false accusation due to a grudge. It is also reported that Huang Jingchu, using a false name, dared to come to court for questioning the other day. The court held that his false accusation was based on evidence and immediately sent him to prison for questioning.

Electoral Dispute in the Seventh District: An electoral dispute occurred in the election of the township head of Weixiang Township in the seventh district of this county. The former township head, Luo Ji Sanfen, submitted a request to the province and county for investigation. Yesterday, the Provincial Department of Civil Affairs ordered the county to investigate and verify the matter.

Wuxi 85

A Rural Woman Hanged Herself: Yang, the wife of Jin Gui, the son of Jia Heshang, a farmer in Nanmiaoqiao Village in the sixth or seventh district (Jingyun Market), has been married for three years and has a daughter. Recently, Yang suddenly had suicidal thoughts. She secretly hanged herself in the room the day before yesterday. The next morning, the father-in-law discovered that she had died. The village head, Sun Bao, learned of the incident and reported it to the county court at 2:00 PM to request that someone be sent to the village for an autopsy. The prosecutor's office reported the matter and sent Prosecutor Du to the village with Shen, the coroner, and bailiffs to perform an autopsy in accordance with the law.

Ding Shuangsheng Recruits Shareholders to Repay Debts: The debt dispute of Ding Shuangsheng Silk Shop on Dashi Bridge in Wuxi City has not been resolved. It is learned that a creditors' meeting was held at the county chamber of commerce again at 2:00 PM yesterday afternoon. More than 100 creditors attended. Chairman Qian Sunqing made a speech, stating that Ding Shuangsheng's existing inventory of goods, accounts receivable, and business assets, as well as the funds owed by Jiu Sheng Jiang Fengyi, should be collected first and distributed equally among the creditors, so that the creditors can recover a portion of their debts first, and the rest can be recovered from Ding in the future. All the creditors agreed. Next, they discussed the issue of auditing the accounts and decided to have two people from the depositors and creditors, one person from the Zhuang family, one person from the silk and cloth industry, and one person from the chamber of commerce to jointly audit the accounts. There was no objection from the public and it was approved. Next, it was resolved to request Ding Shuangsheng to submit the cash flow and classified account books from the years of the Republic of China 15 to 19. The creditors and the silk and cloth industry commissioned the county chamber of commerce to recruit all the inventory and assets of Ding Shuangsheng in order to repay a portion of the debts.

Judgment on the Nan Tang Overturned Ship Case: On February 14, the Yuanyi small steamer of the Taili Shipping Bureau in Wuxi overturned in Nan Tang due to overloading passengers, drowning passengers Mi Hefang and others. Subsequently, the families of the deceased organized a joint association and repeatedly negotiated. The county court also conducted multiple investigations. It is learned that yesterday was the date for the judgment of this case. Yang Xiangqi, Xiang Sanshi, and Lu Xingsheng, who were in custody, were brought to court. At 5:00 PM, Judge Yang Jian took the seat in the first court and announced the judgment. Yang Xiangqi was fined 500 yuan for causing death due to negligence in business. Xiang Sanshi was sentenced to four months of imprisonment. Lu Xingsheng was found not guilty. The attached civil lawsuit was transferred to the civil court for trial.

Changzhou 86

The Drowned Male Corpse Was Found to Have Been Poisoned: A nameless male corpse was found in the Zhang Huangqiao River in the seventh district of Wu County, Nanzhou Township. After the district office reported the case, the county court sent a police chief and others to perform an autopsy. There were no wounds on the body, but the gums and fingernails were purple, indicating that he had taken poison before falling into the river. It was suspected that he had been murdered. Yang, the chief prosecutor, was informed and, considering the seriousness of the case, went to the scene again on the 18th to conduct an autopsy in order to investigate and handle the case.

Nine Bandits Were Executed by Firing Squad: Zhang Pengzhu, the county magistrate and director of the Clearing the Countryside Bureau of Wu County, previously reported that he had interrogated the bandits Zhu Aren, Zhi Xilin, Zhu Sanda, Zhang Qi, Gu Rongsheng, Sun Linchang, Lu Zhongfu, Zhang Dai, and Xiao Yang Ruichang, and they had all confessed to the facts of their crimes. He immediately proposed the death penalty and submitted it to the provincial government for approval. Chairman Zhang was informed and dispatched police to bring the nine bandits Zhu Aren and others to the scene at 9:00 AM on the 18th. After verifying their identities, they were tied up and taken to the Fengweidun execution ground to be executed by firing squad.

Changshu 87

Road Construction Workers Repeatedly Cause Trouble: Since the Zhenhu Long-Distance Changtai section started construction on the 6th of this month, there have been frequent reports of road construction workers causing trouble on various pretexts. On the 14th, workers in Guli Village, First District, incited by others, smashed the shops and residence of Zhen Leader Xi Ke. Fortunately, Xi escaped from the roof and was not beaten. After the Zhen Leader reported to the District Office, which forwarded the report to the County Government, on the 16th, Jin Minjun, a section chief from the County Government, along with Chen Qiwei, the head of the Construction Bureau, and an assistant from the First District, went to the countryside to investigate and earnestly persuade the workers. However, after Jin and his team arrived in the countryside, they received another report stating that Yang Yuqian, the head of Hujing Township, had gathered four or five hundred workers at his home, claiming they wanted to tear down the Yang family's house. After asking someone to mediate, Yang gave six jugs of white wine as compensation to the workers, and the matter was settled. Similarly, at the home of Xu Zhisun, the head of Dalu Town, three or four hundred workers gathered, claiming they wanted to eat meat and drink wine, or else they would tear down the house. At that time, Section Chief Jin and Bureau Chief Chen went to persuade them, but without effect. Later, Qu Liangshi (the owner of the Tieqin Tongjian Lou library) was invited to stop them, and the matter was finally resolved.

Bandit Leader Zheng Yushan Arrested and Sent to the County: Zheng Yushan, a native of another province, had been operating in Wangshi Town, Fushan District, in this county, as a pier boss. Two years ago, he was arrested by the county on suspicion of being a bandit. He was subsequently released on bail by merchants. In reality, Zheng was a notorious pirate leader, specializing in directing secret operations in the interior. Incidents such as the kidnapping of Zhang Chengqi and Zhang Baoqi, traditional Chinese medicine practitioners in Xiyang Town, and the robbery of the Xu Zhang family in Tangfangqiao, were all committed by Zheng Yushan's gang. After Zheng Yushan was released, he went into hiding in Shanghai, making it difficult to arrest him. Previously, due to internal strife within the bandit gang, a captured bandit confessed to Zheng Yushan's residence in Shanghai. Zhu Shunqing, the head of the county's investigation team, telegraphed Xu Fengshan, an investigator stationed in Shanghai, to secretly investigate. In early this month, Investigator Xu, together with Li Huchen, the captain of the Wusong Jiangsu Customs Anti-Smuggling Brigade, arrested the bandit Zheng on the 17th and brought him back to Changshu for trial by the County Judiciary.

Nantong 88

Negotiations Over Japanese Ship Sinking Cargo Ship: The Japanese ship Yijin Maru sank Xu Huiyuan's cargo ship in the river off Nantong's Ren Port. On the 17th, party and government agencies held a meeting to discuss and decided that the County Government, together with the Fourth District Chief of the Water Police, should petition the Department of Civil Affairs to forward the petition to the Provincial Government and then to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for serious negotiations. On the other hand, the County Party Department convened local groups to discuss aid measures.

Pingchao District Chief Sentenced to Four Months: Zhang Kui, the District Chief of Pingchao, was accused by Wu Yuru of abuse of power and unauthorized detention. On the 17th, the Criminal Court sentenced Kui to four months in prison for the crime of illegal detention. Both the prosecutor and Zhang stated that they were not satisfied.

Committee Assigned to Survey the Yangtze River Channel: The Ministry of Communications sent Song Xishang, the director of the engineering department of the Yangtze River Channel Improvement Committee, together with Chen Su, the chief of the water conservancy section of the Construction Committee, and Mi Lusi · Stupe, an engineer from the Naval Hydrographic Office, and a party of four, arrived in Tong on the night of the 16th. On the 17th, they went to the riverside area to survey the water flow and used a boat to measure the channel and river flow.

Zhenjiang 89

Forgery of Documents for Extortion Exposed: Dong Shenyuan, a resident of Gaozi Township, was approached a few days ago by two people who claimed that someone named Fang had an important matter to discuss with him at the Deyue Lou in Longjiang Lane. Shen went to the Deyue Lou to meet Fang, but they did not know each other. When Shen asked why, Fang said that someone had reported him to the Security Bureau for communicating with bandits, and that a secret organization was located at No. 20 Xiaojie. Fang said that he had inquired at the Security Bureau and confirmed that this was the case. Fang claimed to know Long Section Chief, Secretary Xie, and Wen Section Chief at the Security Bureau, and that they knew about this matter and that an arrest warrant would soon be issued. Shen asked who had reported him. Fang said it was Dai from the County Party Department. Fang said that he had asked Wen, Long, and Xie to delay the case, and that a response would be received tomorrow (referring to yesterday). Shen asked where to get the response tomorrow. Fang said he would still be at the Deyue Lou at noon. Yesterday afternoon, at about 1:00 PM, Shen went to the Deyue Lou and saw Fang come with a person who introduced himself as Wen Section Chief from the Security Bureau. He confirmed that Dai had indeed reported Shen, but that Wen Section Chief could find a way to resolve the matter, but it would cost 1,000 yuan. Shen asked who the plaintiff was and how the report was made, asking Wen Section Chief to explain the details so that he could understand the truth. Fang then took out a piece of paper from his pocket with the words "Zhenjiang County Party Affairs Reorganization Committee" on it. The salutation was addressed to Li Mingyang, the head of the Security Bureau. The letter stated that Shen was communicating with bandits in the countryside and asked Li to arrest him immediately. After reading the letter, Shen hid it in his pocket and refused to return it. He then announced the gist of the letter to the crowd in the Deyue Lou, causing a commotion. Fang and Wen realized that Shen had seen through their scheme and immediately ran downstairs. Shen chased after them to the end of Jiajia Lane, but Fang had already disappeared. Only Wen was caught and taken to the Qijingling Seventh Precinct Police Station. This morning, the Seventh Precinct Police Station transferred him to the General Bureau for interrogation.

Preparations Begin for Central Bank Branch: The Shanghai Central Bank considers Zhenjiang to be the capital of Jiangsu Province and finds it necessary to establish a branch there. Preparations are actively underway, and Lu Xiaobo, a local gentry, has been hired as the bank manager, Jin [blank] as the chief accountant, and Wu Guixuan as the chief clerk. The address is tentatively planned to be the old Asiatic Petroleum Company site on the riverbank or the Guangzhao Guild Hall.

Rugao 90

Guards Flee with Weapons: Tao Hongbang and two other members of the defense corps of Zoujiaqiao, Zhentao District, Rugao County, fled on the night of the 13th with two box guns and extorted 200 yuan from the Dong family in Zhangjiaqiao, Motou. This was discovered by local villagers, who flew to the Dashijiazhuang defense corps and the public security station to report it. The team leader, Zhao Chengxiang, upon hearing the news, led his team to the area north of Dashijiazhuang Zhangjia Village, where they saw three people walking towards them in a panic. Zhao ordered them to stop for inspection. The three, seeing the situation was not good, opened fire. Zhao also ordered his team to return fire, immediately knocking one person down. The other two managed to escape. It is said that the deceased was Shao [blank]qiao, a member of the corps named Tao Hongbang who fled with weapons. The district office has already disarmed the entire corps and placed the squad leader and corps members under guard, and has reported to the county for instructions.

Ningbo 91

Security Team Arrests Three Important Bandits: The special task force of the Fenghua security team arrested three important bandits, Gao Wenming, Gao Kuanxue, and Gao Deming, in the Tiantian Slope area yesterday based on a report from the People's Newspaper store. Xiaoshan 92

Jiashan 93

Defense Corps Arrests Kidnapper: The urban area defense corps learned on the 11th that a fugitive local bandit named Shen Xiu was hiding in the Yaozhuangqiao countryside. They immediately dispatched a team to arrest him, capturing the bandit and escorting him back for interrogation.

A Suspicious Wife-Killing Case: Shao Atu, a resident of the Ding family's house on Shaoxiang Street in Xitang, was a temple worker at the Sacred Church. On the night of the 4th, at about 10:00 PM, he returned home and, finding that his wife, Ding, was not in the house, went out to look for her. At the entrance of Jiangjia Lane, he found Ding leaning against the wall, barely breathing. She died shortly after being moved. Atu reported this to his fellow villager and police officer Shen Shenqing, who carried the body back. However, the landlord refused to allow the body to be kept in the house, so he hired a boat to transport the body to Dingzha Township, where he notified the deceased's relatives to come and prepare the body for burial. Recently, it has been rumored among the townspeople that the deceased had often quarreled with Chen Sanguan's wife, who was Atu's lover, due to jealousy, and that Atu strangled the deceased with his hands. The town's public security bureau, upon hearing this, summoned Shao Agui and others to the case for investigation. According to Zhang Xu, the deceased was chatting with her in her shop at about 9:00 PM that night before leaving and showed no signs of illness. Ding Songqing, a relative of the deceased, said that Ding's abdomen was swollen when she was prepared for burial and that there were no signs of injury. Shao Atu's testimony was evasive. Therefore, Director Yu, considering that the case involved human life, sent Shao Atu to the County Court on the 16th for trial.

Educational News Highlights

Academic Delegation to France Faces Minor Delays 94

褚民谊 Sends Letter Explaining That the Trip Can Proceed on the 25th of This Month: There have been conflicting rumors regarding the academic delegation to France. Some say that the French members are not following the instructions of the delegation leader, Chu Minyi, and that three crawler vehicles were damaged in an accident, making it impossible to proceed. Yesterday, a reporter from the Guowen News Agency went to the Chinese-French National Institute of Technology to inquire about this matter and learned that Mr. Chu Minyi sent a letter to Mr. Nong Yaomin of the school, describing the situation in detail. The letter stated that the seven crawler vehicles were imported from Tianjin and that it took ten hours to travel from Tianjin to Beiping, and that it took two days to travel less than a hundred li from Beiping to Changping County, which shows how delayed the trip was. However, this was because the roads around Beiping were too bad and there were too many loose rocks. These vehicles are more suitable for traveling in deserts and on land. The report in the Ping Bao that the vehicles fell into the river is completely false. The vehicles weigh seven tons, so they cannot travel quickly. The rubber bands on the front and rear wheels are specially made and extremely strong, but unfortunately, these rubber bands were not properly packaged when they were shipped from France to Tianjin, so they were exposed to the heat and humidity of the tropics and the Mediterranean Sea, which caused them to lose their elasticity and the rubber tires were damaged. Thus, extremely strong materials became fragile and were damaged by small stones when traveling through Changping County, making it impossible to proceed. The vehicles are currently parked 15 li outside of Changping County, and French workers are repairing them. The French representative, Bu An, has telegraphed the Citroen repair factory in Paris to send new rubber bands via the Siberian Railway to Beiping. It is estimated that these rubber bands will arrive in two weeks and that the trip can proceed on the 25th of this month. As for the report that the French were acting independently and that our side sent personnel to the French Embassy to question them, these are all false. The crawler vehicles did not display national flags because they were not prepared in time. This matter was explained by Yu (Chu Minyi referring to himself) to the French representative, Bu An, in Shanghai. Yu said that he would have many national flags made in Shanghai and bring them to Beiping for the delegation to display. Therefore, the French side did not prepare them. The speculations circulating outside are confused and cannot be believed. In short, developing the Northwest is an urgent task, and it is necessary to start with transportation. Yu is therefore determined to move forward despite the dangers and will definitely travel to Xinjiang to conduct on-the-spot inspections to plan for the development of transportation in the Northwest and to seek the development of Chinese industry.

Jiangsu Department of Education Orders Qualified Teachers from the First Certification to Quickly Obtain Licenses 95

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education has issued an order urging elementary school teachers who passed the first certification last year to quickly obtain their licenses. It has been found that many elementary school teachers who passed the first certification last year have not yet obtained their licenses. It has been almost a year now, but no one has obtained a license, which is not in accordance with the regulations. The current certification examination is about to be held, and further delays will not be allowed. In addition to issuing separate orders, this order is being issued again to urge the bureau chiefs to instruct all elementary school teachers to quickly follow the statutory procedures to come to the department to obtain their licenses so that the matter can be concluded. This is of utmost importance.

Jiangsu Department of Education Revises the Validity Period of Certification 96

The Jiangsu Department of Education has issued an order to the education bureaus of various counties to investigate the temporary standards for the validity period of certified elementary school teachers in Jiangsu Province previously promulgated by the department. Articles 3 and 4 stipulate the conditions for extension in order to be cautious about teacher qualifications. However, since the implementation of these standards, elementary school teachers in various counties who are truly excellent in teaching and have outstanding achievements are often unable to obtain the qualifications because the provincial supervisors have not conducted thorough inspections, resulting in the regrettable loss of talent. In order to remedy the aforementioned shortcomings, paragraphs C of Articles 3 and 4 of the original standards are hereby amended. Paragraph C of Article 3: Has been inspected by provincial supervisors or provincial experimental elementary school local education instructors and county supervisors education committee members. Paragraph C of Article 4: Has been inspected by provincial supervisors or provincial experimental elementary school local education instructors and county supervisors education committee members and has received two or more excellent evaluations. The order is being issued to notify the education bureaus of the changes.

Normal University and Women's Normal College to Merge 97

Beiping, 19th: The Normal University and the Women's Normal College will merge next year. The administrative departments of the two schools will be fully unified. This year's graduates of the school will set off in two directions, northeast and southeast, to visit.

Fourth District: The Fourth District Education Association of this city convened a general meeting of members at the Guangzhao Public School on North Sichuan Road on the 15th, with Zhong Quan, a representative from the City Party Department, and Yao Zhibi, a representative from the City Education Bureau, providing guidance. The National Society for Children's Education Annual Meeting First Day 99

| Opened Yesterday Morning | Dong Renjian Presided | Xu Peihuang, Chen Heqin, et al. Speak

Grand Opening Ceremony 100

The second annual meeting of the National Society for Children's Education opened at the Shanghai Municipal Council North District Elementary School at 9:00 AM yesterday. More than 250 members of the society attended. Xu Peihuang, the director of the City Education Bureau, Yang Weiyu of the National Vocational Education Society, educators Zheng Xiaocang, Liu Tingfang, Shang Zhongyi, and others were present. Dong Renjian presided over the ceremony according to etiquette. The chairman reported that today is the opening of the second annual meeting of the society. This meeting was originally scheduled to be held in Suzhou, but it was changed to Shanghai due to the convenience of transportation. The history of the society is very short. In 1926, a small number of comrades were interested in early childhood education and organized the Kindergarten Education Research Association in Nanjing. Later, because the meaning was too narrow and the scope was too small, it was changed to the Children's Education Society. In 1929, the inaugural meeting was held in Hangzhou. Last July, the first annual meeting was held in Wuxi. Now, the second annual meeting is being held. The number of members has gradually increased, with 25 group members and 500 individual members. In terms of funding, in addition to the membership fees paid by the members, the Ministry of Education also provided a subsidy of 100 yuan this year. As for the career, the Children's Education Monthly is published every month, and there are plans to publish an annual report. Due to time constraints, the society cannot have a large performance in society, and it cannot keep up with the educational groups of various countries in the world. It is hoped that it will be able to publish series of publications in the future and make efforts in experimental education for children, and that experts will provide guidance and various institutions will assist in cooperation, so that careers can be developed. In addition to inviting educational experts to give lectures, there will also be achievement exhibitions, performances, and receptions from various agencies. It is hoped that all members attending the meeting will participate. Then, Xu Peihuang, director of the City Education Bureau, gave a speech, saying that he was very honored to be able to participate in the annual meeting of the Children's Education Society. Those of you who come from various provinces to discuss children's education issues will surely have remarkable achievements in the future. Shanghai is a major trading port with the attention of both Chinese and foreigners, and educational career is very important. The results of your discussions will surely give us a lot of reference. Your society has only been established for two or three years, and its achievements are already so great, and the future is immeasurable. I would like to congratulate you all first and hope that you will work hard in the psychological construction of the Premier to train children to have good personalities. The Party and the country are very fortunate. Then, Chen Heqin, representing the Shanghai Municipal Council and the Education Committee of the Public Concession, extended a welcome to the members attending the meeting on behalf of the Education Office of the Chinese University. Then, Yang Weiyu, representing the National Vocational Education Society, gave a speech, saying that the two American educators, Dr. Dewey and Dr. Monroe, came to China to visit and criticized China's primary education as being no less than that of Europe and the United States. Japanese educators also came to China to visit and had the same thoughts. This is enough to show the progress of Chinese children's education. However, those who do not understand education often say that we only know how to copy and adapt the laws of the East and the West. We do not think this is right, but we will definitely merge Chinese and foreign education into one furnace and then create an education method that is suitable for the new China. Then, the psychologist Liu Tingfang gave a speech, saying that in the past, China only knew how to imitate the education methods of Japan, the United States, and other countries and had no creative spirit, so there was no progress from father to son. In the future, we should create Chinese education. Then, Zheng Xiaocang gave a speech, saying that according to recent research on the meaning and trends of children by Thorndike, the learning of adults is the same as that of children, but in terms of children's education, it can be extended from the age of six in elementary school to kindergarten and infancy, so the meaning and scope of children is greater than that recognized by ordinary people. At the same time, the issue of children's education has been recognized by educators in various countries, but we should not only pay attention to children's education, but also pay attention to the education of children's parents, so that parents can understand how to protect and educate children. Therefore, children's education should not only educate children, but also extend to children's parents. Also, we should pay attention to practice when studying educational fruits, but theory is also very important, so it is hoped that the society will not only study from the practical aspects in the future, but also take into account the theoretical aspects. Finally, the chairman gave a thank-you speech and invited Ms. MandRrenleci, an American educator, to give a speech. After the speech, the members had lunch at the Jiande Savings Society. The meeting opened at 1:30 PM. First, Huang Yi gave a speech on several methods of recent research on children's thinking. The teacher of the French Elementary School of the French Concession spoke on the teaching methods of kindergartens and elementary schools, and his secretary, Shen Zhonghe, represented him at the meeting to speak.

Jinan University to Establish Two Campuses in Beijing and Shanghai 105

School Affairs Meeting to Be Held at 3:00 PM This Afternoon

Jinan University has become famous in recent years, and the number of overseas Chinese students returning to China has increased sharply. The Zhenru campus is really not enough to accommodate them. It is expected that even more students will return to China this summer, so the university has applied to the Commander-in-Chief of the Army, Navy, and Air Force for permission to return the Jinan campus in Xuejia Lane, Beijing, so that it can be used exclusively for junior high schools. The university has received an instruction from the Commander-in-Chief: "I have received your report. I will order Yang Jie, the commander of the Ningzhencheng Song Four Roads, to investigate and order the relocation." The university sent another letter to Commander Yang yesterday to expedite the investigation and order the relocation, and appointed Zhang Jialu as the receiving committee member. Starting from the 20th academic year, the junior high school department will be moved to the Beijing campus for training and divided into departments in Shanghai. The Department of Law on Laoshenfu Road will still be moved back to Zhenru.

Also, it is reported that the 17 members of the Lushan Collection Group of the Department of Biology of the university, led by Dr. Gao Chongkui and Dr. Su Rugan, have been busy with collection work in the mountains in recent days, and the results are no less than those of Tiantai Mountain last year. The university will also hold a school affairs meeting at Hua'an Building, 8th Floor, at 3:00 PM this afternoon.

Opening of Shanghai's First Long-Distance Race 107

| 10:00 AM This Morning | Starting Next to the Chen Ying Shiles Memorial Tower in Ximen | -

The Shanghai Education Bureau's first long-distance race, which stirred the entire city, opened at 10:00 AM this morning. The courage and eagerness to be first of the racers lined up in a row, and the excitement and cheers of the audience were as expected. The following is a brief account of the situation:

Venue Arrangement: The venue is located under the Chen Ying Shiles Memorial Tower, surrounded by bamboo fences and decorated with colored decorations. A couplet is prominently displayed, reading: "Brave and strong children strive to be the first, circling the city twice, washing away the shame of the sick man of East Asia. Magnificent scholars promote and guide with one heart, Shanghai sets an example to promote the spirit of the Chinese nation."

Awarding Location: Many people from all walks of life have enthusiastically sponsored and donated prizes for this conference. The organizing committee has designated the awarding ceremony to be held at the Fanguangqiao Republican Cinema, taking into account its proximity to the memorial tower and its factual convenience.

Important People Attending: In addition to Chairman Zhang (Mayor) and his wife, representatives from the City Party Department, directors of various bureaus, and representatives from various groups and institutions must attend the opening ceremony and the award ceremony. It is now recognized that promoting sports is the most important thing to do.

Route: The route of the race will follow the three-road circle, circling twice, which has been announced earlier. It is reported that the direction of the route is from the memorial tower in the south, passing through Laoximen, Shangwenmen, Dananmen, Xiaonanmen, Dadongmen, Xiaodongmen, Xinbeimen, Laobeimen, Xiaobeimen, and then back to the memorial tower, and then repeating the circuit.

Maintaining Order: In addition to the police from the Public Security Bureau being dispatched to isolate vehicles from driving through the various places, the Boy Scouts of the East Asian Sports Academy are also invited to maintain order. The position of the patrol chief is held by Qu Yue, a teacher at the school.

Enthusiastic Referees: Many of the referees for this competition are well-known figures in the Shanghai sports community. It is heard that they have agreed to arrive at the venue before 9:00 AM today to prepare everything.

Eager Racers: The conference is to promote the idea of a general increase in physical fitness, so it has set the number of winners at 15. Those who can complete the race in one hour outside of the top 15 will also be given souvenirs, so 256 people have signed up to join in a short period of time, and it is expected that they will arrive on time and strive to be the first.

This Year's Annual Marathon Race 111

Tentatively Scheduled for May 24th

Requesting Sponsorship from All Parties Regarding Funding Issues

Whether this year's annual marathon long-distance race should continue to be held has attracted general attention. The Shanghai Westerners' Amateur Sports Association therefore convened a special meeting to discuss this matter. It was resolved that if sufficient financial assistance can be obtained from all parties and competitors actively participate, then this year's annual marathon long-distance race will continue to be held, tentatively scheduled for May 24th. The meeting will reconvene next Friday to formally decide whether or not to hold it. The meeting proceedings are briefly described below:

All Parties Actively Preparing. A total of eight people attended the meeting. The Amateur Association President, Mr. Blackridge, chaired the meeting and stated that there were many requests to continue holding the annual marathon race. However, economic factors, the venue, and the presence of participants were all prerequisites. The French garrison representative stated that their army could contribute ten people. The Schouder army also had four or six participants. The Russian team had about eight people. Lei Midiqi stated that the Chinese team was also actively preparing and could have about fifteen participants. The Chinese team conducted a long-distance race from Shanghai to Suzhou the day before yesterday as practice.

Economics are a Major Problem. Since there is no concern about enthusiastic participation in the competition, the next issue is economics. The various expenses for the competition require approximately 250 yuan, plus 500 yuan for prizes. There is no source for these 800 yuan in funding. Therefore, it was unanimously resolved to proceed with fundraising.

Next Meeting to Decide. The next meeting is scheduled for Friday. All parties will separately collect the results of their fundraising efforts. If economic problems do not arise, then a decision will be made to borrow a venue and solicit participants.

Li Maochong Fails in Shanghai's Advanced Marksmanship Competition This Year 112

| Last Year's Champion Becomes Runner-Up |

Defeated by Portuguese Man, Meidina

Score: 1440 to 2000

Li Maochong, last year's Shanghai Advanced Marksmanship Competition champion, rejoined the battle this year and eventually reached the final against the Portuguese man, Meidina, who was the last person Li defeated last year. Before the final match at the Victoria Club, Li was highly favored. However, once the match began, Meidina soared while Li repeatedly made mistakes, ultimately losing and becoming the runner-up. As a result, Meidina won this year's championship with a score of 2000 to 1440.

World News Briefs 114

— Hai Ke

▲ According to a recent survey by British sociologists, there are 296,000 widowers aged 30 to 34, 375,000 widowers aged 35 to 44, 394,000 unmarried women aged 30 to 34, and 548,000 unmarried women aged 35 to 44 in England.

▲ According to a survey, the telephone management system worldwide is most perfect in Spain, even surpassing England and the United States.

▲ The birth rate in England has been declining recently. It is said that there are two main reasons: one is that urban life is too unhygienic, and the other is that men advocate for marrying late.

▲ Among the five continents in the world, the graves of British soldiers are located in almost 111 countries, with the most in France and Belgium during the European War, totaling more than 550,000 graves.

▲ Miss A.M. Swift, a blind student in England, is proficient in Braille shorthand and can write 120 words per minute. She won an award in a test at the London Chamber of Commerce.

▲ American tourists spend 60 million gold pounds in Europe each year, with France receiving the most.

Remembering Mr. Yuan Hanyun 115

— Chen Yuanliang

Mr. Hanyun was the second son of former President Yuan Weiting. He was known as a talented scholar of his time. He passed away at noon on the 22nd of last month at his residence at No. 4 Liangyi Alley, Tianjin, at the age of only 42. Literary friends in Shanghai were saddened by the news. Today, we are holding a memorial meeting for him. Mr. Hanyun was born with intelligence and could memorize anything he saw. He was particularly skilled in poetry and prose. His father doted on him, and all official documents were drafted and transcribed by him. His calligraphy was elegant, and those who obtained it cherished it as a treasure. His poetic talent was overflowing, reaching the level of Wen Tingyun and Li Shangyin. He also painted and once drew a Kunqu opera script. From a young age, he was fond of Kunqu opera and Peking opera. He often invited Da Bao to talk about plays, and Xu Ling taught him “Touring the Garden, Startling the Dream” and "Qin Tiao." Comic plays such as “Examining the Head, Stabbing the Soup,” and “Small Banquet, Disturbing Studies” were often performed, and he was very popular. In the winter of the sixteenth year, at the invitation of the China Road Association, he borrowed the Shanghai Gongwu Stage to perform “Examining the Head” with Ouyang Yuqian and the Tiangang attendants. I personally saw him put on makeup and act as Tang Biaobei, a hunchbacked yamen servant in the play. His humorous performance made people laugh. In addition to acting in plays, he also spent much of his time with female performers. Whenever beautiful women surrounded him and music filled the air, he would be inspired and reciprocate with gifts. There are many anecdotes about him. Kunqu opera singer Wang Biyun was once appreciated by Mr. Yuan. Mr. Yuan knew she could write and asked her to inscribe on a Ming Dynasty palace woman's rouge box and gifted it to her. The box was less than an inch high and less than two inches in diameter. It was carved with countless pavilions, flowers, and birds, with as many as seven layers of carvings. However, when viewed, it looked like a flat mirror, perfect for storing rouge. What he exchanged was only a few words, but he may have regarded it as precious because it came from the hand of a beautiful woman. People in the brothels thought he was noble and talented and enjoyed being close to him. When he found someone he loved, he would bring her home with a generous dowry. It is said that he had as many concubines as there were hairpins, but after a long time, his love faded, and they would separate. In the end, only a few remained. He had experienced the bitterness and joy of life. Usually, his descriptions of literature about flowers were vivid, truly worthy of the "dripping powder, kneading cream, blowing fragrance, and chewing nectar." For example, the couplet he gave to Chu Xia said, "I was already interested when I first met you, let alone moved the wine closer to my eyebrows and held your hand when climbing the building. Xia Qi became a dress but I still hated that it was colored, wishing to cut clouds into slippers and tread the moon as a plate." It was very similar to the concept of a beautiful pearl. In addition to loving poetry, books, lyrics, and music, Mr. Yuan also liked collecting antiques. He wrote "Collection of World Coins," a two-volume book full of rubbings of currencies from past dynasties, with detailed annotations, making it a grand view. In the past, I received a draft of "Zhuchen Ji" from a friend, which was like an antique catalog. He classified it with an example and prefaced it, saying, "When I was young, I understood the love of ancient books and strange paintings, and I lingered and couldn't leave. When I grew up, I bought them a little. Occasionally, I would show them to connoisseurs and study them carefully. The things I have obtained over the years have increased to more than a hundred. I am afraid that they will be forgotten and scattered over time, and I am worried that there is no way to tell future generations. So I will narrate the categories of what I have collected." Mr. Yuan was uninhibited and did not adhere to trivial matters. He was addicted to opium and often painted while smoking day and night. If a friend visited, he could meet even if he was sharing a pillow with a concubine. He was so open-minded. Later, he quit his addiction and returned to Tianjin in the autumn of the seventeenth year. He never touched opium again after quitting, and his weight increased. We hoped that he would make good use of his talent and often offer pearls to the literary world. Who knew that this farewell would be a farewell forever? Alas!

Elegy for Hanyun 116

— Zhao Nantian

Gained a wild reputation like Du Sijiun, after all, Yuan Si was also outstanding. Ten thousand deaths in the rivers and lakes, with twin green temples (In the year of Jiazi, Hanyun returned north and sent a poem saying, "Ten thousand deaths in the rivers and lakes, I will come and go.") A lifetime of career with several red skirts. Willing to use sorrow and joy to dispel silk and bamboo, exhausting the quality of Qinshu to buy drunk. Such talent, such a passing, only Lord Xinling in the nine springs.

The Future of Humanity in My Ideal 117

— Dunjin

In ancient times, people were very tall and lived very long lives. Fangfengshi was nine acres wide, and Pengzu lived to be 800 years old. Later, they gradually shortened. Now, people are getting shorter and shorter. Living to 60 or 70 years old is considered old. This still refers to our predecessors. I don't know what will happen in the future. According to my ideal speculation, people will slowly become dogs, sheep, cats, and mice. Then, the size will reach the extreme and will be no different from insects. The ephemeral may be the embodiment of the old saying "the sky is turned upside down." (Not paid)

A Small Cigarette Factory in Beiping 118

— Qiushui

Near the front gate of Beiping, there is a small cigarette factory located at the entrance of a shop. The shop displays a variety of cigarettes and has a hand-cranked cigarette rolling machine used for manufacturing cigarettes. The factory owner, Mr. Liu, is both the owner and the worker. He also hires several children who specialize in picking up cigarette butts on the roads everywhere to supply the raw materials for the factory. Because the tobacco used in this small cigarette is not fresh tobacco, but rather collected cigarette butts that have been re-rolled. Every day, Mr. Liu orders the children to pick up the cigarette butts that have been abandoned by people everywhere and pays a very cheap price. He also sorts the collected cigarette butts to prepare for manufacturing. The butt cigarettes (new term) sold in this factory also have various brands, and the prices are not uniform. For example, if you want a "Galiaoke" or a "Platinum Dragon," you can ask him. He will put the cigarette butts of the same brand that you choose into the cigarette rolling machine and roll them for you. In a moment, the cigarette is rolled. After paying the price (about two copper coins at most), you can smoke it. Mr. Liu's cigarette factory has been open for several years and has always had good business, earning a lot of money. Mr. Liu himself started out as a cigarette butt picker, so he has a lot of research on this way.

It is common to see cigarette butt pickers in large cities with a cloth bag and bamboo tongs patrolling the streets. They collect a lot and sell them to small cigarette companies for manufacturing ordinary cigarettes to sell as new cigarettes. Mr. Liu's plan is even more appropriate, selling them at low prices by category. This is his ingenuity, and it is no wonder that he is making a small fortune.

— Yucen

This time, the Sino-Japanese Exhibition exhibited many products from collectors and artists in Shanghai, and there was also a visiting group to promote national art. The relationship is sincere and great. At the same time, Zhang Shanzi and Daqian, the owners of Da Fengtang, also took their families to Japan on the 18th by boat. Shanzi has recently been busy with painting affairs and has been suffering from guiding students. He goes to bed late every night and feels that his tongue is dry. The doctor advised him to rest. Therefore, going to Japan will be mainly for rest and travel. The mountains and rivers of Fusang will relieve fatigue and medicine. It is estimated that he will stay for two months. At the Sino-Japanese Exhibition, he is indeed an exhibitor of new and old paintings, but he does not intend to join the group to socialize. The packed paintings include landscapes by Zhao Songxue and Tang Liuru, flowers and figures by Shitao, and several recent works by the two gentlemen. They can be called a thousand-foot sword. Da Fengtang's collections and works have a great reputation at home and abroad, and are far-reaching in Chicken Forest. It is unnecessary to wait until today. In the second month of Jiangnan, the spring water is green. It is expected that the two floating beards will cross with the sea sail. It is no different from the boat. Li Guo hopes like a fairy. The Vigor of the Advertising Industry 120

— Songlu

In recent years, there has been an excellent phenomenon in my country regarding the great development of industry and commerce, that is, the sudden vigor of the advertising industry. The majority of well-known business companies also know to shift their eyes to the publicity of text and art, and hire experts at high salaries to take charge of their affairs, and are even willing to sacrifice huge amounts of money to allocate as regular expenses. Advertising companies that specialize in serving industry and commerce have also sprung up like mushrooms after rain. We only need to observe the progress of the news industry in recent years to associate this with advertising, which is closely related to the news and has helped it.

I have been engaged in advertising research as far back as eight or nine years ago, only because few people in the business world at that time could pay attention to this way. In fact, the majority of business companies did not have considerable faith in the effectiveness of advertising promotion. Therefore, I shifted my efforts to writing and engaged in the news industry. However, my interest in advertising research has never diminished. Last year, I responded to the invitation of a large company here and returned to Shanghai to specialize in advertising. With more contact, my interest in advertising research has become stronger, and my friends such as Xu Zhuodai and Ni Gulian have also abandoned their writing careers and engaged in advertising writing. Yesterday, Mr. Kuang Xiaoan invited me to drink. After drinking, Mr. Kuang asked me about my recent situation, so I wrote a couplet to ridicule myself: "The iron inkstone has been worn through, and there is still some love left for advertising; the silver pen has been written bald, and there is no more mood for writing." Although the sentence is funny, it is also a little bit of emotion.

Recently, new advertising initiatives include rickshaw advertising, utility pole advertising, and traffic advertising companies that exclusively package train advertising on both routes. The Meilingden Company contracts the body advertising of trolleybuses. Competing for novelty and victory can attract general attention. For example, the Xianling Company uses the power of radio broadcasting to give speeches and report advertisements. Within a minute, the effectiveness of the advertisement can be broadcast to the whole country, which is also amazing.

As for newspaper advertising, it has also progressed compared to before. Not only is attention paid to text, but also to the study of art. Judging by the exquisite advertisements in pictorials, it can be seen. It is expected that ten years later, newspapers will rely on the help of advertising to sell more widely, and advertising will rely on the power of newspapers to achieve greater results. Although the price of advertising sacrifices will be greater, the number of households reached will be greater. According to my personal speculation, after ten years, the advertisement rate for each inch of newspaper will be calculated at three yuan, which is an inevitable fact.

Travels in India (29) 121

— Linghua

Mr. Zhang Xiangcheng from Yunnan and Jamyang, a Tibetan, came to visit. The Tibetan wore a red mandarin jacket and had cut his hair. I could not understand his language, so Mr. Zhang translated for him. He is in the Tibetan Department of the Asiatic Society here. This society has people from all Asian countries, including Chinese, and there were Russians, but not now. It is a genuine academic organization that is set up for archaeological research and the culture of various Asian countries. It was originally a social organization, but now it has obtained assistance from the British government and is of a semi-official nature. However, its purpose is academic. I heard that the chairman is Dutch. These kinds of things must be started and organized by gentlemen, and the effect will be long-lasting. There is the Geographical Society in Beijing, China, run by my old friend Zhang Xiangwen, which still exists today. I previously met a Swede in the north who specialized in researching northern Chinese animals and collected many kinds of small snakes, even several boxes, sent by their society. Sweden is a small country, but they have come to China to collect small snakes. China is a big country, but they do not know how to unite to study their homeland's cultural relics. It is truly shameful. Rituals are lost and sought in the wild, and learning is in the four barbarians. This is true.

On the 14th, I talked with an Indian friend about something that surprised me. Professor Mala Tai pointed to a passerby and said to me, "This kind of person eats beef. Think about it, the cow plows the field for me and provides milk for my whole family, young and old. Its merit is no different from my wet nurse. I have already eaten its strength and eaten its milk, how can I bear to kill and eat its meat? These people can eat beef, they have no conscience." I asked how many vegetarians there are in all of India. Bimalananda Bramchari replied that there are many meat-eaters in Calcutta because Westerners eat meat and there are many Muslims. If you remove these provinces, most of the Indian Hindus in other provinces do not eat living things throughout India. I think Hinduism is so noble and loves even insects and ants. Zhuangzi said that all things are one with me. Its asceticism is greater than Buddhism. Indians can be the world's masters, noble Indians. I now understand why Indians are inconvenienced to open restaurants because people of different religions cannot eat together and have many taboos.

The Indian view of life takes the highest virtue as the standard, so they despise physical happiness and believe in fatalism. Wealth, poverty, longevity, and heaven are all destined, and there is no divorce in marriage. A wife never remarries after her husband dies, but a husband can remarry after his wife dies. Although new trends have risen, divorce is difficult to implement in India.

I see that Indian paintings contain divine meaning everywhere, especially women. They have a kind of ethereal and distant spirit. They have the true, the good, and the beautiful. Many paintings depict husbands as monks rejecting women or cultivating the Tao and staying away from women. This is the Indian view of life.

The police are like the Indian police in Shanghai, China, with red turbans and long poles, very quiet. I see people standing and watching a paper card, and they do not ask. The house number system is very bad, the characters are small, and it is very inconvenient to visit friends. The strangest thing is that the numbers go from 1 to 50 on the right street, and then return to the right street from 51 to 100. It is very bad. The house number system in Shanghai is very good, and Nanjing is the most effective. The British and American systems are not good.

The government interferes with printing quite strictly. If I print a speech, even if it is only a few pages, the name of the printing house must be printed on it before it can be published. However, the meetings and speeches of various circles are still free.

Gold Prices Finally Decline 122

Decrease… Eight Taels Four Qian

The Atmosphere is Extremely Anxious. Yesterday, the 18th, the gold price fluctuated slightly. It was weak in the morning, then stabilized, and finally weakened again, falling by more than eight taels. The state was confusing and difficult to grasp. There were five or six taels of trading in between, and people were anxious and at a loss. The main reason was that each firm was buying and selling. The price of silver on the international market fell very little, causing the gold price to open lower. Moreover, there were more sellers than buyers. Later, after breaking 710 taels, large households took the opportunity to step in and re-energize the price, rising by six or seven taels. Before the exchange rate was even listed, the transaction price was already loose. By noon, the selling pressure suddenly intensified, and the price was difficult to support, falling with the current. After failing again by seven taels, the market closed as usual on Saturday. It is expected that the main contract will have to rebound this morning. During this week, it happened to be the rollover period, and the June contract, from Thursday to today, had a maximum price of 724 taels and a minimum price of 703 taels. There was also a difference of 21 taels in just three days. Comparing the total with the first opening price, it fell by thirteen or fourteen taels.

Frequent Changes Discovered. Yesterday morning's opening price was 711 taels and five qian, a decrease of three taels and four qian. The main contract only fell by one-sixteenth recently. The distant contract and the price of silver were not affected. There was no change in the European market, and the United States was also waiting to see. Moreover, the private telegrams rose by one-sixteenth. Therefore, people's hearts were down. Zhifeng Yonghongli, Wupin, and others were the first to sell. In just over ten minutes, it suddenly fell to 05 taels and five qian. Soon after, Shunli, Qianchangxiang, Wanxingyu, Da, and others all bought. Moreover, Holland absorbed 136,875 June gold, which was sold by Mitsui, Sumitomo, and others. Therefore, it returned to two taels, totaling 08 taels and one qian. First, an order was issued not to move when it was 06 taels and eight qian to 08 taels and five qian. Yuan Mao Yong and others bought it. Suddenly, Hengxing went on the market to sell a small amount. The various firms also sold, so they were pressed down by two taels, to about 06 taels at around ten o'clock. Later, HSBC and others absorbed 6875 July gold, and the price was pulled up by three or four taels. After ten thirty, it had broken out of 710 taels. Yuan Mao Yong, Qianchangxiang, Shunli, Wanxing, Bingxingchang, Yuyong, and others made progress. At eleven o'clock, it was 12 taels and six qian. Not long after, retail investors sold, and because the bank sold 13,625 to 6875 June gold, it was suppressed to 11 taels, two or three qian. For a moment, buyers were still diligent, and at eleven thirty, it was 13 taels. Later, the exchange rate was loose and not good. Especially, Yongheng, Yuanxingyong, Yuyuda, Yuanheng, and others tended to sell. In an instant, people's hearts were empty, and seekers retreated, so the price fell by six or seven taels, all the way to the closing price at noon, which was only 06 taels and five qian, a decrease of eight taels and four qian compared to the previous day, and was suppressed again to 05 taels. The maximum price in half a day was 13 taels, and the minimum price was 05 taels and five qian, a total of seven taels and five qian. Looking back at the Wupin morning market, it was 11 taels, and the noon closing was 05 taels and eight qian. The price was still 765 taels, a total of 58 taels to 52 taels, and then 59 taels. The registered price was 05 taels to 07 taels, and the water supplement was 01 tael.

Intricate Ins and Outs. The transactions between colleagues were complicated. Yuan Mao Yong, Cheng Feng Yong, Chang Sheng Yong, Yuan Tai, Bing Xing, Wan Xing, Shun Li, Fu Chang, Yuan Heng, Qian Chang Xiang, and Cui Chang Yong all bought in. Yu Da initially entered and exited. Later, Chun Yuan Yong, Fu Tai Heng, and Da Feng Cheng exited very tightly. Zhi Feng Yong Hong Li, Yi Yu, Heng Xing, and Sheng Da were all selling short positions. Finally, Yong Heng and Yuan Xing Yong also sold. Speculators occasionally had deposits and withdrawals. Traders sold when they made a profit. Guangbang was shorting with more than 2,000 contracts. Dalian was still long, adding more than 2,000 contracts, then exiting more than 1,000 contracts.

Foreign Exchange Turns Loose 123

Yesterday, the British and American silver markets were very flat, but the exchange rate fell. HSBC's listing in Shanghai did not change at all. The bank's buying and selling prices were initially flat and then weak. The gold market was already weak and had broken into 710 taels. Therefore, the exchange rate at noon was weaker. As for spot sales, although there was no significant improvement in volume, there were still some small transactions among various groups, and the sales of fine yarn were smooth, with market prices tight. Last Week US Cotton Turned Weak 133

Buyers Were Cautious Due to Rising Prices

The weather is suitable and planting is smooth.

New York, 17th, telegram report on the raw cotton market in one week. The cotton market gradually turned down last week because traders' purchases were blocked by rising prices, and the weather in the south was again suitable, causing bulls to close positions again, and planting was progressing smoothly. Securities also did not improve, and the Liverpool market was also poor. Cooperatives sold May contracts and bought further-out months. Trading was quiet, and people in the industry were waiting for more accurate news on this season's cotton fields and new cotton. There is an optimistic argument in Washington that the total amount of world cotton production this season is estimated to be 25.5 million bales, compared to 26.3 million bales last year. Based on this number, the rolling inventory of US cotton at the end of the season will be huge, and the non-thinness of other inventories is knowable. Agricultural Bureau Chairman Si Dongjun declared that cotton planters who want to hope for satisfactory cotton prices must reduce cotton fields by at least 25%. Flour Price Stays Firm 136

Yesterday, in the flour market, after the opening of the morning and afternoon markets, the market for each month generally trended toward stability. Because the quoted price of foreign wheat rose by one or two jiao, the hearts of outsiders were inevitably reactivated. Although the Tianjin gang had returns in the middle (it was heard that sales in Tianjin were fatigued and the price was lower by two and a half fen), the market trend remained very firm. This was because the factory tightened the recent pricing of foreign wheat, and the exchange rate could not be determined for a while. Therefore, although buying interest did not surge, the asking price resumed to a better step. As a result, this month was better by five mils than the previous day, May was better by seven mils and a half, June was better by five mils, July and August were better by one fen, and September was better by one fen and two mils.

Wheat Futures Market Turned Steady Afterwards 137

Yesterday, in the wheat futures market, after the opening of the morning and afternoon markets, the market for each month presented a first flat and then firm appearance. Initially, because the floating multi-positions in the inland were successively returned, although the near term was not good, the distant term had been slightly raised due to the good news of foreign wheat. Afterwards, because the flour market was very stable, the buying interest of outsiders gradually revived. The key to this was that the price of foreign wheat could not be determined for a while, and gangs from Hankou and Qingdao, etc., if they were to draw again, still had the potential for continued shipment. Therefore, the market could not help but be stable. As a result, this month was better by two fen than the previous day, May was better by one fen, June was better by three fen, July was better by two fen, August was better by two fen, and September was better by four fen.

Chairman Chiang Returns to Nanjing Last Night 144

Condolences to Xiong's Injury Yesterday Morning

Chairman Chiang and his wife were originally scheduled to go to Nanjing tonight, but at around 8 p.m. last night, they suddenly ordered the captain of the guard Wang Shihe to book a train car with the Railway Bureau. They took the night train to Nanjing at 11:45 p.m. last night. Very few people knew in advance, and those who went to the station to see them off were only Chen Xizeng and Jiang Yi, the deputy director of the adjutant's office of the garrison headquarters. The security near the station was still handled by public security bureau police officers. The military band of the garrison headquarters also went to the station to play music. Those accompanying were two secretaries, Ding and Mao, and the captain of the guard Wang Shihe, and more than 30 guards.

Chairman Chiang and his wife went to Kong Xiangxi's residence on West Endes Road at 11 a.m. yesterday for lunch. After the meal, they rested briefly and took a car to tour North New Jing. They returned at 2:30 p.m. and went to Xiong Shihui's residence to express condolences for Xiong's injury and talked for about half an hour. Then they returned to their private residence on Jiaerye Road. Li Zhonggong, the general manager of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, went to visit but was not seen. At 4 p.m., they went to the Song residence on Seymour Road to meet with Yu Qiaqing and others.

Yesterday's Election Situation 147

General Supervisor Inspects: Yesterday, 21 labor unions in Pudong, Zhabei, and Fahua districts held voting with excellent order. Hou Dachun still received the most votes yesterday. The British American Tobacco Company's union has 8,000 workers. The factory originally did not allow workers to participate in the election, considering it would interfere with work hours. However, the municipal authorities insisted, and the factory had no choice but to cooperate with the election office yesterday to distribute ballots to the workers for writing, and then collect and deposit them into ballot boxes, so the order was excellent. General Supervisor Fan Zhengbo and Clerk Feng Liutang went to the Zhabei Baoshan Road Commerce Labor Union to inspect, and the order was the best, with Boy Scouts on site to maintain order.

Chamber of Commerce Strives for Universal Suffrage for Merchants 158

National Federation of Chambers of Commerce Asks the National Government for Relief

The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce received a telegram from the Beijing General Chamber of Commerce yesterday, which stated: "To the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce of the Republic of China: We received a telegram from the Nanjing Central Party Headquarters and the National Government's National Assembly Election General Office, which stated: 'To the Nanjing Central Party Headquarters and the National Government's National Assembly Election General Office: We hereby present a copy of the letter from the Nanjing Municipal Chamber of Commerce requesting relief because merchants were suddenly deprived of their civil rights during the upcoming national election. We have read the report in the Beijing Municipal Election Office's report on March 31st that the Beijing Municipal National Election Office telegraphed the General Office the day before to explain four points of doubt. The reply was: "The first item states that the Chamber of Commerce should use the representatives of its affiliated trade associations and the direct members of the Chamber of Commerce's stores as electors, and there is no need to limit the age." We were shocked to learn of this. Restricting the merchants' due right to vote and distinguishing them from other professional groups concerns the merchants' personality, so we must request relief. We are now submitting three points to request a clear explanation. Please consider them: (1) Merchants and workers are on an equal footing. Workers who join the labor union have the right to vote, while store employees are also merchants, but they are restricted if they join the trade association. Those who are not representatives of the trade association cannot have the right to vote. The national regulations should not have such unfair provisions. This is the first request for clarification. (2) The regulations of the industrial and commercial trade associations stipulate that companies and firms in the same industry may be members of the trade association, while the detailed rules stipulate that each company and firm may send one person, and only those who have more than ten employees can recommend one store employee representative, and at most, no more than three. The intention is to regulate labor and capital by adjusting the number of main parties and the number of employees. However, although the users are not direct members of the association, they are indirectly members of the association. The store employees have the right to vote as store employee representatives, but the entire store employees who elected the representatives have no right to vote. It is not known under which regulations the restrictions are based. This is the second request for clarification. (3) For example, if a company has ten workers and ten store employees, the workers have one vote each, while the store employees cannot have one vote unless there are ten of them. Compared with each other, the workers are in a superior position, and they will actively participate in the election at the time of the election, while the majority of the store employees have had their right to vote deprived. As a result, they will become passive about the election, and no one from the business community will be elected. Although they are participating in name, it is only a formality. Why should the business community be included in the election? This is the third request for clarification.' Based on the above three points, merchants should strive for the right to vote. Now, the various associations in the city have come to the association to request that Prime Minister Sun Yat-sen's advocacy of civil rights is that the larger the organization, the thicker the power. Merchants and agricultural workers are in the same position, and store employees are also merchants. The first National Assembly election will strictly restrict and narrow the scope. In the future, merchants may never have a basis for foothold. Not only will they cancel their inherent qualifications, but also deprive them of their due human rights. The matter is unfair, and the group is deeply angry. We dare to state the reasons and request your office (government) to review and quickly correct the meaning of the previous explanation and give all merchants the opportunity to participate in the election in order to provide relief and show great fairness. We await your instructions and obey them." With this as the standard, it is felt that the merchants' efforts to succeed in the National Revolution are great. The merchants are the taxpayers, and all supplies are taken from our merchants. The current election regulations are far less than the workers in the comparison. It is difficult to accept. Please allow to clearly order the correction, stipulating that all merchants have universal suffrage, delete the representative provisions, and show fairness to the law. The Beijing General Chamber of Commerce's cold seal.

The association specially telegraphed the National Government yesterday to ask for help, which is recorded as follows: "To the National Government in Nanjing: A telegram from the Beijing Municipal Chamber of Commerce said that the application for the relief of merchants being deprived of the right to vote in the election. In addition to the cold-day telegram application, the corresponding telegram requests assistance. It is stipulated that the workers' right to vote is granted upon joining the membership, while the merchants' right to vote can not be granted unless it is the right of the voters. Therefore, the right of merchants to be elected and the equality of the election should be considered, and the uniformity of equal treatment should be the whole nation. To the Federation of the Chambers of Commerce.
